[01/10/21, 1:12:42‚ÄØPM] Sonny Sadhwani-CREAI-Agent: EMBASSY STATEMENT 

There are certain rumours and false information being fed through social media regarding the Embassy Group‚Äôs acquisition of Le Meridien Hotel in Bangalore. There is no truth and factual basis for these information.  
 
Le Meridien Hotel property is owned by Mac Charles (India) Limited, which is a company listed on the Bombay Stock Exchange. The Embassy Group acquired the majority of the shares of Mac Charles from its erstwhile owners by way of a block trade on the BSE in February 2017. The Embassy Group has complied with all applicable laws, rules and regulations, including applicable timelines, while acquiring these shares for valuable consideration being paid in full. As such all  amounts payable due to the erstwhile owners of the shares (including shareholders who were members of the general public) of Mac Charles (India) Limited (including shareholders who were members of the general public) were paid by the Embassy Group through the BSE in full and there is no amounts due as falsely propagated on the social media. 
 
Since inception, our governance framework emphasises on accountability, transparency and integrity and we continue to work on these core values.

*EVERYTHING*
The Name is the *BRAND*

*CREA (I)* is a Brand.
Lets value it, everytime we write it, say it or publicise it. Don't write CREA or Crea or other variants. Write CREA (I) only, consistently.

CREA (I) is a part of *NAR India* which is a National Brand. Value it please üôèNot NARI , not NAR-India, but NAR India. Its pronounced as NAR India and not as NAAR as lot of people do.

This is Convention Year. Lets wear our pride on our sleeves and respect our  Organisations with correct Branding.

Thank you üôèüôè
